	KSR_communist_korea_independence = {
	
		visible = {
			AND = {
				country_exists = DPK
				DPK = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
		
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				date > 1948.9.9
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				KOR = { country_exists = yes is_subject = no NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = US_KOREA } }
			}
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						DPK = { is_subject_of = SOV }
					}
					DPK = {
						remove_country_leader_role = {
							character = DPK_terenty_shtykov
							ideology = stalinism
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						DPK = { is_subject_of = PRC }
					}
					DPK = {
						remove_country_leader_role = {
							character = DPK_gao_gang
							ideology = stalinism
						}
					}
				}
				else = { }
			}
			DPK = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
			end_puppet = DPK
			give_guarantee = DPK
			DPK = { give_military_access = ROOT }
			
			if = {

			}

				DPK = {
					remove_country_leader_role = {

						ideology = stalinism
					}
					remove_country_leader_role = {
						character = DPK_gao_gang
						ideology = stalinism
					}
					promote_character = KOR_kim_il_sung
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = communism
						last_election = "1936.1.1"
						election_frequency = 48
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
			}

		}
	}
